   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">2011 Davis Cup</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <table class="infobox vevent" style="width:22em">

      <p> The <b>2011 <a href="/wiki/Davis_Cup" title="Davis Cup">Davis Cup</a></b> (also known as the <b>2011 Davis Cup by BNP Paribas</b> for sponsorship purposes) is the 100th edition of a tournament between national teams in men's tennis. Spain was the championship team, winning the final over Argentina, 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The draw took place in September 2010 in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>, Belgium.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Group_Play-offs">World Group Play-offs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Davis_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: World Group Play-offs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: 
       <a href="/wiki/2011_Davis_Cup_World_Group_Play-offs" title="2011 Davis Cup World Group Play-offs">2011 Davis Cup World Group Play-offs</a>
      </div> 
      <p><i>Date: 16–18 September</i> </p>
      <p>The eight losing teams in the World Group first round ties and eight winners of the Zonal Group I final round ties will compete in the World Group Play-offs for spots in the <a href="/wiki/2012_Davis_Cup_World_Group" title="2012 Davis Cup World Group">2012 World Group</a>. </p> 
      <div> 
       <table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">
        <tbody>
         <tr> 
          <td style="width: 50%;text-align: left; vertical-align: top;"> <p><b>Seeded teams</b> </p> 
           <ol>
            <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_Davis_Cup_team" title="Czech Republic Davis Cup team">Czech Republic</a></li> 
            <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Russia_Davis_Cup_team" title="Russia Davis Cup team">Russia</a></li> 
            <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="660" data-file-height="480">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Israel_Davis_Cup_team" title="Israel Davis Cup team">Israel</a></li>

      </ul> 
      <p>Honduras and Jamaica finished in the relegation places. However, in 2012 Groups III and IV were merged, so no demotion occurred. </p>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_I_3">Group I</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Davis_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Group I">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
